msg:Location is at 10 minutes DiDi ride from the French Concession where the most of the restaurant and bars are located and same distance from the Bund.
Our room was comfortable but the hotel is surrounded by high traffic elevated road, the "white noise" of the cars could be hear at the lower floors, luckily we were at the 23rd floor.
The window of our room looked on the opposite side of Jing'An park and the view was nothing special, only with the dark it improved a bit.
Gym is equipped with new training equipment but not enough for deadlifts (no barbell), not equipped for bench press neither for weight row.
Price of beverages at "long bar" absolutely expensive (108 RMB for 1 Corona...), 150 RMB + for any other cocktail.
Breakfast at buffet is nothing special: the second day I have ordered a full egg omelette and I got a white egg one, tasteless and pretty raw. 
Food selection at buffet for breakfast not satisfactory at all for me, poor selection of jams, yogurt, bread, cakes, no oat/soy milk available.

üè®I booked a basic room without breakfast (the main point is to save money, and reviews generally indicate that breakfast is not good), but because the basic room looks like... I wrote down the reason why I came to stay with the idea of ‚Äã‚Äã‚Äã‚Äãtrying it out, but I was surprised to be informed of the upgrade when I checked in. Go to the signature [Classic Room].
üè®The hotel was built in 2009. It not only popularized the concept of "urban vacation" in China, but also became a "model" for countless imitations of the same type. But it is said that "it has always been imitated and never surpassed". When you stroll around the hotel and hit the horse stakes at the door, you will see the same "gold brick" as the Hall of Supreme Harmony under your feet. The 33-meter-long tree trunk is used as the hospitality/entertainment space. Old objects, the silk in the sliding door... some seem to have lasted a hundred years, while others have a new generation style. The ancient charm and contemporary design blend seamlessly, forming a unique and uncompromising sense of luxury and comfort.
üè® The guest room has a Chinese-style entrance, and the interior decoration follows the same style (indeed, when you come in, you will find that this space layout is imitated by many hotels of the same type that you have stayed in before), with exquisite lacquerware and antique porcelain embellished throughout. The polished teak floor is very comfortable to step on with bare feet. The metal parts are a bit old and there are some bumps on the cabinets, but it doesn't matter. I think the guest room has just the right balance between signs of use and careful maintenance.
üè®A room with a view, exquisite welcome fruits, a free mini bar, and most importantly, a comfortable bed (the first time I slept in a hotel with a firm bed that I loved)...all of this is reminiscent of Somerset Maugham's The description of a good hotel: there is a bathroom with a bathtub that you can lie down in, and a deck chair on the balcony that you can lazily lean on. This is civilization.
üè®The staff are all warm, polite and considerate, responsive to requests and at the same time very discerning and efficient. It is very, very difficult to still maintain the original intention after 14 years of operation.
üè®As far as a one-night experience is concerned, I can‚Äôt comment at the moment (of course, because I didn‚Äôt try the food and didn‚Äôt use the fitness and swimming facilities). I‚Äôm really satisfied, and I finally understand the reason why many qualified people only choose to live here when they come to Shanghai.

msg:It is located next to Jing'an Park and is positioned as a city resort hotel. The car passes through the rows of bamboo trees on both sides before reaching the entrance of the hotel, giving people a feeling of starting a vacation. The new Chinese style of the lobby is very pleasing and attractive. The bar counters in a row to the end of the lobby are divided into different functional areas. The hotel reception, bar, afternoon tea, Chinese chairs and sofas are designed in a unified and elegant style.
The room space is good, there is a sofa resting place and a small table, the bathtub with a view is the highlight, the only point is that you can hear the noise outside when you sleep in the evening. I booked a view room facing Jing'an Park to see Jing'an Temple. It should be a selling point, but the soundproofing is not good. At night, I hear the sound of traffic on the road. Intermittent but non-stop is really a problem for me who wants to sleep quietly.
The breakfast buffet in the middle of the night was delicious, and I ordered Chinese and Western staples. It's free to look at the green scenery of the park outside.
Health facilities are the strengths of the hotel. The indoor swimming pool with its own landscape and the jacuzzi in the changing room, dry and wet steam and ice mist shower can really kill an afternoon. My own spa is also famous in Shanghai, you can make an appoin**ent to enjoy it when you have time.
The service is really good, the front desk, housekeeping and even the switchboard are very good, and the attitude is kind.
If there is no noise at night, it should be possible to score a five-star score. Recommended.
